Kidnapped Hostage Released After Ransom Paid: The son of Chen Zhaofu, a farmer in Wangtianli Village, Wenyong Township, Third District of Wuyi County, has been kidnapped by bandits for many days. Zhaofu entrusted someone to negotiate with the bandits in Laoguqiao and agreed on a ransom of 1,350 yuan. 1,150 yuan was paid, and 200 yuan was still owed. The payment date was agreed upon. After the payment, the bandits sent the hostage out by the riverbank there the night before and said that they were not afraid that you would not pay the owed money.

Yangzhou

The case of Feng Suqing being abducted still requires a retrial. In this city, Yao Tianlin from outside the city managed to marry Feng, whose maiden name was Suqing. In August of the year before last, she was lured and abducted to Fengtian by her friend Liu Dianxun to work as a prostitute and sold for 600 foreign dollars, and her name was changed to Liu Yueqin. Yao suddenly received a letter from his wife stating the circumstances of being lured and sold into prostitution by Liu. She now wants to return to Yangzhou but cannot. After receiving the letter, Yao submitted a document to the county government and the Public Security Bureau requesting that Liu be arrested and interrogated. When Liu was summoned for interrogation, he firmly denied it. Later, after someone provided bail, the county government sent a letter to the Fengtian court requesting that Feng Suqing be summoned for questioning. It was confirmed that Liu had abducted her. A reply has now been sent to the county, and the county government has transferred it to the court for handling. It is now known that the court reconvened the original plaintiffs and defendants today (the 21st) for a hearing. Unexpectedly, the defendant did not appear, resulting in no outcome. It is said that the presiding judge instructed the plaintiff, Yao Tianlin, to return and wait for Liu to be arrested before further interrogation.

The Court Investigates the Education Bureau's Stolen Document Case. Previously, due to the case of the Jiangdu Education Bureau's junior high school account books being stolen, the Public Security Bureau and the county government repeatedly interrogated Chen Shusen, the document management officer, and Pan Da, a clerk. Subsequently, County Magistrate Chen recorded the confessions and sent the above three people to the court prosecutor's office for a hearing. Yesterday (the 20th), Lu, the prosecutor in charge of the case, accompanied by a clerk and bailiffs, went to the Education Bureau to conduct an on-site inspection, and took the handkerchief, screw starter, and other items left by the document thief to the court as an aid to the investigation. This was in the morning. In the afternoon, the prosecutor's office reopened the court and released Pan Da, who was considered to be more suspicious, on bail. Around 6 o'clock, Zhou Yangzhi, a secretary in the county government, was suddenly arrested. When Zhou was arrested, the bailiffs believed that Hou Maolin, who lived with Zhou, was obstructing official duties and hiding the defendant. Prosecutor Lu then separately prosecuted these two crimes in court and ordered Zhou's detention. Zhou's family then went to Principal Bao's home at the junior high school to make a scene. Bao then went to the court to request that Zhou be released on bail pending trial. Prosecutor Lu met him and told him that Zhou's suspicion was serious and that he could not be released on bail. If he had any opinions, he could state them in court. Today (the 21st), Prosecutor Lu again led police officers to Principal Bao's home and Zhou Yangzhi's residence for separate searches. The case is now being accepted and tried by the court.

Danyang

Reactionary Suspects Arrested. Xu Xianhan and Rong Yousong, residents of Shangde City in this county, have been reported for suspected reactionary activities. County Magistrate Shen has ordered the Director of the Public Security Bureau to arrest Xu and others for interrogation.

Bandits Attempt to Rob the Beijing-Shanghai Train, Causing Disaster. The night before last, when the Beijing-Shanghai night express train arrived at Xinfeng Station, bandits lurking at the rear of the train threatened to stop the train in an attempted robbery. When that failed, they shot and killed a baggage handler and wounded a train guard. After the incident, they jumped off the train to escape, but fell and fainted due to the speed of the train. The train stopped at the station in this county. The garrison troops stationed at the station rushed to the scene, found the bandits responsible for the incident, and sent them to the provincial capital for interrogation.

Jingjiang

Sending Personnel to Rugao to Negotiate Bandit Suppression. The county government believes that bandit suppression is difficult because this county is adjacent to Rugao County. It plans to send Secretary Ge Tianyi to negotiate.

Bandits Surrendering One After Another. Notorious bandits Bian Tangyu and Zhang Er and others have been looting in partnership at Xibaimuqiao and Sidunzi on the border between Jingjiang and Taixing. Now that Li Jigeng and his like have already surrendered themselves, they have also gone to the Taixing County government, found guarantors, and surrendered their weapons.

Hangzhou

Civil Affairs Department Appoints and Dismisses Three County Magistrates. Cheng Zhenjun, the Zhejiang Provincial Committee member and acting Director of the Civil Affairs Department, has paid close attention to the county governments and is particularly strict in examining the diligence of the county magistrates. At the recent 348th Provincial Government meeting, he proposed to replace three county magistrates, which was approved. Feng Shimo, the current magistrate of Qu County, will temporarily act as the magistrate of Yuqian County (the magistrate of Yuqian County, Shen Naigeng, has been detained by the court for a corruption case). Xu Zhigui is appointed as the magistrate of Qu County. Zhao Baoqing, the magistrate of Tangxi County, is dismissed and investigated, and Li Zheng is appointed on a probationary basis.

A Daytime Robbery Occurs at the City Station. Li Xilin, a partner in the Changxing Printing House in Hangzhou, ordered Xie Zhaosong, the shop's clerk, to withdraw 50 foreign dollars from a draft at the city station post office yesterday. After Zhao Song withdrew the money from the post office at 3 PM, a bandit named Ding Lida suddenly rushed up, grabbed the banknotes from his pocket, and fled. Zhao Song grabbed him and shouted for help. A police officer heard the call, stepped forward, and arrested him. After interrogation by Huang Zucheng, a staff member, it was revealed that there were three accomplices: Li Honggen and Chen Yunsheng, all residing at No. 22, Huayang Hotel at the City Station. According to the confession, Huang sent Inspector Miao and Police Officer Zhang to investigate and arrest them, but they had already fled. That night, the bandit was sent to the Public Security Bureau for handling.

Ningbo

Chairman Chiang Scheduled to Return to Fenghua. Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the National Government, will return to his ancestral home in Fenghua on a fixed date to inspect his family tomb and survey the Yin-Feng Highway. Jiang, the supervisor of the Ou Hai Customs, and Mao, the Director of the Ningbo Public Security Bureau, also went to Nanjing to inquire about the date of his trip. According to news from Nanjing, Chairman Chiang originally planned to return to Zhejiang immediately, but because all sectors of the capital have scheduled a welcome rally for his triumphant return today (the 22nd) and require his personal attendance, he has decided to go from Nanjing to Shanghai tomorrow (the 23rd) and then take a boat back to his ancestral home in Fenghua.

The Security Corps Attacks a Large Band of Bandits. Since the anti-rebellion case occurred in Fenghua County, the bandits have become rampant and widespread. Three hundred bandits even swarmed to the Cai area the other day, with rumors spreading of an impending attack. Upon receiving this news, the county government ordered the Security Corps to mobilize various squads from all directions to suppress them. At Cai, they found more than 300 bandits, all armed with guns, no different from a regular army. The bandit leaders, Qiu Wenqing, claimed to be the commander of the newly formed Sixth Division; Chen Shunchang claimed to be the commander of the Third Brigade; and Sun Libiao claimed to be the commander of the Fourth Brigade. They also distributed notices stating their intention to attack the city. However, the bandits' firearms were all short guns and Mausers, making it difficult to fight. When the Security Corps arrived, the bandits fled towards Chen Gongling. The Security Corps attacked from behind, killing three bandits and capturing a bandit scout, Huang Tusheng. After interrogation, he revealed the location of several bandit dens. The Security Corps has secretly searched them.

Letter

Letter from Tian Yueqiu of Yangzhou

To the Editor: Having read the Yangzhou correspondence column in your newspaper on October 19th, which stated that "(Tian Yueqiu, the director of Tianye Hospital, was implicated because a suspected Communist, so and so, testified in court that he had conspired with Tian," this is inconsistent with the facts. The truth is that Yang Disheng, the executive committee member of the second branch of the first district of Gongjin Township in Jiangdu County, was sued in the High Court. After a thorough interrogation, all allegations were found to be baseless and the case was returned to the Jiangdu County Court for investigation into whether there was incitement of others to resist rent. After the county court summoned him for questioning, Yang was ordered to post bail. Yueqiu and Yang had a teacher-student relationship in the past, so Yueqiu acted as Yang's guarantor. On the day of the court hearing, Yang was unable to arrive due to unforeseen circumstances. The judge immediately issued a warrant for the arrest of the guarantor. However, the bailiff, not understanding the case, used a gun to coerce him and handcuffed his hands, acting as if he were arresting a thief. When the judge inquired about the guarantee, he ordered him to submit a deadline for handing over Yang. Yueqiu then realized that he had been illegally arrested. He asked the judge to explain the meaning of the bailiff's use of a gun and handcuffs. After questioning the bailiff, the judge agreed to give him appropriate punishment. This is the truth about Yueqiu's illegal arrest. I hereby submit this letter requesting that your newspaper make a correction to clarify the facts and distinguish right from wrong. Tian Yueqiu, Yangzhou, October 21st.

Important Education News

Ministry Recommends Zhu Jingnong as a Member of the Overseas Student Management Committee

According to regulations, the Ministry of Education recommends one member to the Central Government's Overseas Student Management Committee. Previously, Chen Jian, the director of the Social Education Department, was a member, but he resigned. The Central Training Department sent a letter to the Ministry of Education stating that Chen's resignation had left a vacancy on the committee and requested a recommendation for a successor. The Ministry of Education has now replied to the Central Training Department, recommending Zhu Jingnong, the permanent director, as the successor.

Local News

The Problem of Receiving Labor University

The Ministry of Education Implements a Strict Attitude Toward Receiving

The School Affairs Council Telegraphed the National Government to Send a Principal Quickly

Students Welcome the Receiving Personnel to Arrive at the School

Zhu Baoqin, Xie Shuying, Zhuang Quan, and three other members of the Ministry of Education’s Labor University Inspection Committee stationed in Shanghai, were commissioned by the Ministry as special commissioners to receive Labor University, and ordered to go to receive it immediately. If the school refused to obey and resisted the order, it would be ordered to shut down. The Shanghai Municipal Government also received a telegram from the Ministry of Education, requesting that the police be dispatched to assist Zhu, Xie, and Zhuang, the three receiving commissioners, in handling the receiving matters when necessary.

The School Affairs Council Telegraphed to Quickly Appoint a Principal. The problem of the principal of the National Labor University has not been resolved. The School Affairs Council of the school telegraphed to the government and the executive yuan, requesting the quick appointment of a principal. The full text of the two telegrams is as follows: "To the Honorable President of the Executive Yuan of the Nanjing National Government, Due to the resignation of the former principal of the affiliated school, we have repeatedly telegraphed to your honorable Yuan requesting the appointment of a successor. We are grateful for your examination of the school affairs of the affiliated school, which is now maintained by the School Affairs Council. We are deeply concerned that we cannot overcome the heavy responsibilities and numerous affairs. We earnestly request that your honorable Yuan consider the expectations of all teachers and students of the affiliated school and appoint a new principal as soon as possible, so that the responsibility can be assigned to facilitate school affairs. We await your orders. The School Affairs Council of the National Labor University respectfully kowtows." Ma also telegraphed, "To the Honorable Minister Jiang of the Nanjing Ministry of Education, We previously received Order No. 1042 from your honorable Ministry, dispatching personnel to the school to verify the records. We immediately complied with the order and prepared various forms and registers for verification. Suddenly, this telegram changed the verification to the receiving of the affiliated school by teachers and students, which caused great confusion. They all said that before the new principal is appointed, there is no need to send personnel to receive. We earnestly request that your honorable Ministry withdraw the order to receive and maintain the original verification plan. We pray without end. The School Affairs Council of the National Labor University respectfully kowtows."

Students Welcome the Ministry of Education to Receive. After the Ministry of Education announced the reception of Labor University, the students of the school were extremely excited. Yesterday, the entire student body of the College of Engineering issued a statement expressing their welcome to the news of the reception by the teachers. It was reported that more than 70 students attended the general meeting of the members to discuss the results, and they also expressed their welcome. Later, a small number of people bought out by the school authorities tried to sabotage it, resulting in the inability to publish the news. The College of Agriculture is farther away and the news is later, so there is no statement yet, but according to the news from the students of the college, the majority also welcome the reception by the Ministry of Education and will take consistent action with the two colleges of Engineering and the Social Sciences.

Zhuang Quan Fills the Position of Dean of the College of Engineering. The position of Dean of the College of Engineering of the National Labor University has been vacant for a long time. The affiliated factory of the school has more than ten factories. Recently, Zhuang Quan was hired by the Ministry of Education as the dean. Zhuang graduated from Tongji University and studied at the Dresden University of Technology in Germany, achieving the best grades among Chinese students. He has served as the director of the Hanyang Arsenal, the Northeast Arsenal, and the Machine Factory. He is currently the director of the Machine Factory of the Shanghai Arsenal. Minister Jiang Menglin borrowed him from Director Chen Gongxia for the position.

The Municipal Education Bureau Holds Private School Testing

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau believes that many private elementary schools have been registered. In order to understand the achievements of each school and study the standards of various testing materials, the Testing Section of the Research Department has planned to conduct four standard tests. Ding Zhongxuan, Xu Dingjun, He Yuanzhi, Huang Sen, Shen Yuguang, and Huang Zhen were assigned as testing staff to go to various schools for testing on October 20th. Forty-two schools participated in the testing.

The Municipal Education Bureau Bans the Private Benefit-the-People Free School

Private schools in this city often use the beautiful name of enthusiasm for education to solicit donations everywhere. The Municipal Education Bureau has ordered a ban on file. Now, the Benefit-the-People Obligation School has been accused of false donations to the bureau. The bureau has sent personnel to investigate and found the following report: "The Benefit-the-People Obligation School on Maigen Road, Tonghe Lane, in the British Concession has two female teachers who go to the British and French Concessions to solicit donations from door to door. A receipt was also found. On October 18th, I went to the school to investigate and inquired with nearby residents. I learned that the school has two classrooms and more than 60 students. There are ten teachers and staff members, seven men and three women. The expenses are 1,800 yuan per year. The income is 400 yuan per year in tuition fees, and the rest is donated by female teachers Wang Qin and others. A receipt was found, but when compared with the original receipt, the style was different and the seal color was also different. After repeated inquiries, they insisted that the school only had one type of receipt. It is thought that outsiders knew that the school was going to solicit donations, so they impersonated it. I also found that the content of the school's curriculum was not in accordance with regulations, and the facilities were simple, like a private school. Moreover, the school charges tuition fees and calls it 'obligation,' which is obviously a way to deceive. Furthermore, the school has two classrooms and ten teachers. When I went to the school to investigate, I only saw Teacher Peng Kangnian at the school. When asked about the other teachers, he said, 'Only I teach on Saturdays.' The corruption of the school can be imagined. In this situation, we should send a letter to the Special District Court to strictly ban it to prevent outsiders from being fooled." It is now known that the bureau has decided to do so.

Record of the Third Anniversary Celebration of Shanghai Middle School

Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai Middle School held its third anniversary celebration at the high school department yesterday. The meeting opened at 9:00 AM. The guests included Pan Gongzhan, Standing Committee Member of the Municipal Party Headquarters; Wang Yunwu, Manager of the Commercial Press; Xu Peihuang, Director of the Municipal Education Bureau; Zhu Hange, Representative of the County Education Bureau; and more than 1,800 teachers, staff, high school, junior high school, and experimental elementary school students. Principal Zheng presided over the meeting. First, the school's military band played music to open the meeting. Principal Zheng gave an opening speech, briefly stating that the school paid attention to maintenance in the first year after reorganization, attention to organization in the second year, and attention to improvement in the third year. In the future, special attention will be paid to research and development work. It is hoped that the new school building will be realized as soon as possible, so that the foundation of Shanghai Middle School can be consolidated and gradually developed in the future to become a model middle school in the southeast. Next, guest Wang Yunwu gave a speech, briefly stating the advantages of young people in various countries in the world, and hoping that Shanghai Middle School students could also emulate them. Xu Peihuang briefly stated the relationship between the Shanghai Middle School and the city of Shanghai and hoped to jointly promote the improvement of education in the city. Pan Gongzhan briefly stated that young people's self-cultivation should pay attention to physical fitness, discipline, academics, and conduct at the same time. Zhu Hange briefly stated the relationship between Shanghai Middle School and the County Education Bureau. The school's harmonica team played the harmonica. Finally, Sun Tingsheng, the representative of the teachers and staff, Zhou Hanmei, the representative of the alumni association, and Pang Shunqin, the representative of the students, gave speeches successively. At the end, the military music was played. The entire body took a photo. There was a heavy rain, but the teachers and students of the school lined up for the photo in an orderly manner, which shows the school's daily training. After the meeting was adjourned at 12:00 noon, a dinner was held for all teachers and students, which was a grand occasion. In the afternoon, the high school and junior high school held separate variety shows. There were many programs that cannot be listed. This morning, the junior high school held a Boy Scout review, and this afternoon, the high school students held a military review.

The Third Anniversary Exhibition of Shanghai Middle School

The Shanghai Middle School Experimental Elementary School of Shangwen Road held its third anniversary of reorganization yesterday. At 9:00 AM, all teachers and students went to Shanghai Middle School to participate in the joint anniversary ceremony. In the afternoon, an achievement exhibition and a variety show were held at the school. The achievements were divided into four rooms, mostly teachers' works, full of dazzling things, so beautiful that one cannot take them all in, such as the new school building plan of the administrative department, the century-old savings regulations, the school's economic openness method of the five-power separation, and various regulations and forms, etc. The teaching department's small-problem experimental report, training week implementation report, more than 300 kinds of self-compiled teaching materials for each subject, more than 30 kinds of self-made arithmetic teaching aids, and about 400 wall charts for each subject of party doctrine, national language, arithmetic, natural science, and society, etc. The research department's various teaching records, more than 50 special research reports, the moral cultivation department's more than 30 party doctrine research reports, and more than 20 reading reports are all valuable, so although it was raining, there was a continuous stream of visitors. It is said that the school will continue to display it for one day on the 23rd at the request of Daxia and other schools for visitors to see. There are as many as 20 kinds of variety shows, focusing on the performance of each subject, such as the party doctrine performance of "Riding the Same Boat," the social science performance of the "Sino-Russian Conference," the physical education performance of the "Makeup Pyramid," and the music performance of "Little Painters" and "Three Butterflies," which are even more

Lively, with hundreds of spectators, applause arose from time to time until 8:00 PM when the curtain closed. In addition, the school's three-year general report has also been published, with a price of five dimes per copy, which is rich in content and popular with buyers.

The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center Recruits Industrial Talents to Help Industry

According to the statistics report of the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center last month, there were 782 people who had career talks, and the registrants were 102 from domestic and foreign universities, 46 from vocational schools, 37 from normal schools, 59 from vocational schools, 50 from middle schools, and 9 others. The agencies that entrusted the introduction last month needed more professional talents. Recently, a factory in the city entrusted the center to introduce a draftsman who is skilled in the design of mechanical drawings and specializes in the work of stamping machines, and has more than two years of experience in drawing in an enamel factory. The monthly salary is 30 yuan, providing food and lodging, and can get generous bonuses. A mechanical engineer is also needed who is skilled in the work of stamping machines, has rich experience in making steel molds, and has served in an enamel factory for more than three years. The monthly salary is about 40 yuan, providing food and lodging, and can get generous bonuses. A factory in the city also recruits three apprentices who are 15 to 20 years old, have a junior high school degree or above, and are physically strong. They will graduate in three years. During the study period, a subsidy of 22 to 40 cents per day will be given. When entering the factory, a deposit of 10 yuan and a 2.5-inch photo will be required. A printing company has entrusted the recruitment of two trainees who have graduated from senior elementary school and can endure hardship. Those who are interested in learning can register with the center in accordance with the regulations.

Shanghai Western Football Association Investigates the Suspicion That the Members of the Expedition Team Are Salaried

丨Organize a Special Committee... Please Invite the China Sports Association to Participate丨

The Chinese Expedition Football Team organized by the Yuehua Sports Association originally planned to unite the athletes of Shanghai, Hong Kong, and Singapore to conquer the United States. Later, when the team was waiting for the ship in Singapore, they suddenly received a reply from the British Football Association rejecting them. The team then turned around and returned home. It is said that the reason for the rejection was that the team was suspected of violating the amateur sports. After returning home, the Hong Kong Football Association reviewed Cao Guicheng and Chen Guangyao, two members of the team. As a result, all three had salaried actions and were disqualified from the competition. The Shanghai Western Football Association also discussed this incident at the Executive Committee meeting on the 21st and decided to invite two people from the China National Sports Promotion Association and the association to form an independent committee to conduct research and review the matter. In addition, a chairman should be invited, who should be unrelated to both parties and must be agreed upon by both parties. It is expected that in the near future, whether the Yuehua players violated the amateur rules this time they went abroad will definitely come to light one day.

In addition, the British and American requests to withdraw from Group B and fall into Group C were rejected by the General Assembly.

Hard Court Tennis Tournament to Begin

The Shanghai 18th Hard Court Tennis Tournament will begin on September 1st at the French Chamber of Commerce, with increasing popularity each year. In the past, Lin Baohua, Whitt, Canavero, and Tavoularas have all held the reins and dominated the field. The entry fee is four yuan for singles and five yuan per pair for doubles, regardless of gender. The registration deadline is this month, the 25th, at 6:00 PM.

Party Members Expelled from the Party Lose Their Civil Rights

The Same Applies to Party Members Suspended from Party Rights

The Municipal Government issued instructions to its subordinate bureaus, municipal committee offices, and the Preparatory Committee for the Implementation of the Municipal Organization Law yesterday, stating: "For your information, we have received Instruction No. 3655 from the Executive Yuan, which states: 'We have received Letter No. 15670 from the Secretariat of the Central Executive Committee, which states (regarding the difference between expulsion from the Party, suspension of Party rights, and deprivation of civil rights, and whether those who have been expelled from the Party or suspended from Party rights have the civil rights stipulated in Article 7 of the Law on the Implementation of Township Autonomy, and the right to be elected as the head of a township, neighborhood, or village, please forward to us for review and reply, so that we can instruct compliance). After investigation, Article 81 of the General Regulations stipulates that party members who have been expelled from the Party shall not serve in the government agencies of this party. This meaning was interpreted by the 33rd Standing Committee Meeting of the Third Central Committee in September of the 18th year as being similar to the deprivation of civil rights due to criminal punishment under the criminal law. The reason for saying 'similar' rather than 'the same' is that the reasons and procedures for party discipline and judicial punishment are inherently different. However, in terms of their effect, there is no difference. This is a natural interpretation. Furthermore, the term 'government agencies of this party' includes all central and local government agencies, or local autonomous organizations, such as townships, neighborhoods, and villages, as indicated in Items 1 and 2 of the previous interpretation. There is no doubt about this. While the suspension of Party rights differs from expulsion from the Party, its nature is essentially the same as the restoration of civil rights after deprivation. Therefore, in this regard, the same sanctions should be imposed as on those who have been expelled from the Party, in order to ensure fairness. Furthermore, Article 7 of the Law on the Implementation of Township Autonomy stipulates that citizens of the Republic of China who have been sworn in and registered as township citizens have the right to attend township or town meetings and to exercise the rights of election, recall, initiative, and referendum. The essence of the oath is to swear to uphold the Three Principles of the People and adopt the Five-Power Constitution. Therefore, those who have been subjected to party discipline, expelled from the Party, or are within the period of suspension of Party rights cannot be considered loyal to the principles of this party, and it is difficult to expect them to fulfill their civic oath. It can be inferred that they should not be allowed to enjoy the civil rights of this article. It was resolved at the 110th Standing Committee Meeting of the Central Committee (party members who have been expelled from the Party or suspended from Party rights are no different from those deprived of civil rights and shall not enjoy the civil rights stipulated in Article 7 of the Law on the Implementation of Township Autonomy, and the right to be elected as the head of a township, neighborhood, or village). In addition to being distributed separately, a copy of the case is sent to you for your information and for distribution to your subordinates for their information.' In accordance with this, in addition to distributing it separately, we hereby order the city to inform the lower levels and instruct them to comply accordingly. This is the order."

Garrison Troops Search for Deserters

Nine Deserters Arrested

The Fifth Division, stationed in Shanghai for nearly three years, is well-trained and known to the public for its excellent discipline. Recently, individuals in nearby counties, disregarding the overall situation, have been encouraging soldiers of the division to desert in order to replenish the police force in the counties. Commander Xiong has repeatedly issued orders strictly prohibiting this. However, many soldiers have still deserted to Chongming, Songjiang, Qidong, and other counties. In order to maintain military discipline, Commander Xiong was forced to order Xiong Kexi, the battalion commander stationed in Wusong, to lead the 5th Company of his battalion to Chongming County to search for deserters as a warning to others. Upon hearing that Xiong's battalion was coming, the county had already made preparations, intending to quickly move the police force out of the county seat. Those who came to investigate would hide the Jiangxi police officers (most of the soldiers of the Fifth Division are from Jiangxi). They also feared that a roll call would be taken during the search, so they prepared to hire people to answer in their place. Their intention to collude with deserters is obvious. Battalion Commander Xiong received a confidential report and immediately went to meet with County Magistrate Liang, requesting that the deserters be handed over. Liang refused to hand them over immediately, using the excuse of going to suppress bandits in the western countryside the next morning. Xiong believed that County Magistrate Liang was insincere and led his troops to search the police force. The police initially resisted, but were soon surrounded. As a result, nine deserters were arrested. Afterwards, Battalion Commander Xiong discussed the aftermath with County Magistrate Liang and Long, the captain of the 17th Team of the 4th District of the Water Police. He also dispatched subordinates to patrol the streets to prevent unscrupulous individuals from taking the opportunity to cause trouble. He also gave a speech to the public, saying that he was sorry for the sudden and brief alarm, explaining that he was under orders to search for deserters. Before the troops returned to the City God Temple to rest, he had the company line up for County Magistrate Liang and representatives from various public organizations to inspect the soldiers to see if there was any illegal behavior during the search for deserters. The various public organizations believed that the measures taken were appropriate and praised Battalion Commander Xiong for his quick action. It is reported that the company returned to Wusong to be stationed the day before yesterday.

Zhang Qun Difficult to Decline Chairmanship

Second Day of the Provincial Committee's Discussion with County Training Directors

County-Level Agency Discussion Meeting Held in the Afternoon

Today to Guide the Reorganization of the Chamber of Commerce in Minhang

The Jiangsu Provincial Party Affairs Committee, in order to guide the reorganization of existing mass organizations in various counties, has dispatched Training Director Zhang Yuanyang and Instructor Zhang Renjie, together with Chen Tonggang from the Provincial Department of Construction, to guide the Fourth District counties. After arriving in Shanghai the day before yesterday, they convened the first discussion with the training directors of the various counties at the Shanghai County Party Headquarters. The details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, the discussion continued. Those present included Provincial Training Director Zhang Yuanyang, Instructor Zhang Renjie, Chen Tonggang from the Department of Construction, Han Rongling (Shanghai), Zhu Tiexian (Songjiang), Zhang Ming (Fengxian), Huang Xuze (Qingpu), Ge Zuwang (Baoshan), Wang Guanglong (Chuansha), and Huang Yueping (Nanhui). First, Comrade Zhang Renjie reported, stating briefly the significance of this trip, divided into the following points: (1) Urging the counties to step up their work; (2) The Provincial Government's Department of Construction will send representatives to assist the county governments; (3) Explaining and interpreting laws and regulations and guiding practical issues. Next, he mentioned the mission: (1) Each county is a unit; (2) The Chamber of Commerce should focus on small and medium-sized merchants; (3) Trade associations must complete their organization; (4) Labor unions must be legally organized; (5) Student unions must be organized in accordance with organizational principles and completely; (6) Other social, cultural, and charitable organizations should be guided to establish themselves at any time. Next, he discussed the problems of the counties, hoping to receive a written report to be submitted to the province. He then said that he planned to go to the counties of the Fourth District for actual guidance. Finally, he reported on behalf of the Provincial Training Department, briefly summarizing everything. Next, Chen Tonggang from the Department of Construction reported, saying briefly that he had the same mission as Comrade Zhang, but only to supplement that people's organizations must be organized in accordance with laws and regulations. He was not clear about the Merchants and People's Association and asked the comrades to report so that he could forward it to the director. Next, Provincial Training Director Zhang Yuanjie reported, briefly saying that his department had assigned instructors to go to the counties to step up the work of organizing people's organizations in order to understand the actual situation in the counties. Therefore, he had not participated. He also briefly described the significance: (1) Organizing people's organizations to consolidate the foundation of the Party and government; (2) The people themselves are not urgently needed to be organized at present, but in order for the Party to hand over power to the people, they must be organized and trained; (3) There are too many problems within the Party, and it is generally believed that it is empty and there is no proper party work to be done, so more work should be done to reduce disputes. As for the work, it should be to awaken the people, but empty words are still useless, so it is necessary to go deep among the people. Therefore, the organization of people's organizations is actually opening a path for the Party's cause. As for the purpose of the organization, attention should be paid to the progress of the business. The government supervises, and the Party guides. However, the central plan was promulgated long ago, but so far the results of the work are very few. In order to step up the work, people are sent to do it on the ground. This is the significance of the province sending personnel. At the same time, the government is also paying close attention, so it also sends personnel at the same time, and it can also make the county governments pay attention. As for the purpose, at the very least, the central legislators should not be disappointed. Apply the various rules and regulations to give the people a considerable understanding and interest, and the counties can emulate this. The county training departments should also step up this work. There is great hope. Finally, he reported that the recent work of the training department was quite detailed. (The long speech is not recorded.) Finally, the training directors of the various counties reported on the difficulties in organizing people's organizations. The provincial training director and instructors explained separately, and then the meeting was adjourned. At 2:00 PM, a discussion meeting was convened again with the county-level agencies. Those present were Zhang Renjie (provincial instructor), Chen Tonggang (provincial construction office), Yan Shenyu (county government), Ye Dezhen, Shi She (county education bureau), Wu Wenhua (construction bureau), Ding Guangzhi, Shen Jing'er (public security bureau), Cai Zhongji, Tao Yishan, Wang Libin, Jiang Yanchiu, and Han Rongling (county party headquarters). First, Zhang Renjie reported: (1) The significance of the Party and government jointly organizing people's organizations on the ground; (2) Shanghai will take Minhang as the central area. Regarding people's organizations, the organization should start from there first, and then consider the method of promotion; (3) The funding problem of the Shanghai Farmers' Association; (4) The subsidy problem for reorganizing people's organizations. He hoped that the county government would publicize the laws and regulations on people's organizations as much as possible and post more notices in various places to make the people aware of their importance. Next, the representative of the county government reported, stating briefly that the county had very few public properties, and they had all been designated for use, leaving nothing to spend, so other matters that should be handled could not be carried out due to funding problems. However, the county government had an unshirkable responsibility for the funding problem and would do its best to raise funds, but this would have to wait until the county magistrate returned to Shanghai to make a decision on each case. Finally, two issues were decided: (1) The Farmers' Association should be restored according to the provincial order, and the county government should be responsible for planning the funding for the association according to the provincial standard; (2) The subsidy for guiding the reorganization of people's organizations should be disbursed according to the standard for second-class counties, and the county government should try its best to raise funds. Then it was decided that today (the 23rd), representatives from the county party headquarters and the county government would go to Minhang with the provincial instructors to guide the organization of people's organizations. The meeting was adjourned when the clock struck five.

Proposal from the National Products Industry to the Industrial and Commercial Conference

Wang Jie and An, standing committee members of the China National Products Maintenance Association, were appointed by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce as members of the Industrial and Commercial Conference and are scheduled to go to Beijing on the 31st of this month to participate in the deliberations. The association has already solicited opinions from all industrial and commercial enterprises in Shanghai and appointed committees, including Wang Xingyi, Xu Zouyun, and Xu Chunrong, to conduct a detailed review and classify them. A total of fourteen proposals were made: (1) Regarding the implementation of clothing regulations to relieve the real economy and protect national products; (2) Regarding the abolition of exorbitant taxes and levies to save national products from danger; (3) Regarding relief for unemployed citizens; (4) Regarding strict prohibition of incitement to ensure industrial and commercial stability to benefit workers; (5) Regarding the prompt eradication of banditry to prevent hindrance to the transportation of national products; (6) Regarding the opening of overseas shipping to facilitate transportation; (7) Regarding the adjustment of the burden of commodity taxes to benefit the people's livelihood and maintain national products; (8) Regarding the levying of manufacturing taxes on foreign factories in China and business tax on the sale of foreign goods in the interior, to indirectly prohibit imports and exempt national products from business tax; (9) Regarding the reduction or exemption of export duties on national products and the increase of import duties on foreign goods to maintain national products; (10) Regarding the request to issue industrial bonds of 100 million yuan to establish a basic fund for national product factories; (11) Regarding the promotion of bill of lading financing to facilitate the turnover of industrial and commercial finance; (12) Regarding the request to order the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce to instruct foreign merchants to clear accounts in accordance with regulations and not to arbitrarily delay payments; (13) Regarding the request to exempt heavy taxes on porcelain and dredge transportation rivers; (14) Regarding the standardization of sizes. The association's secretariat has already drafted and submitted the proposals to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for consideration at the conference.

The Shanghai Machinery-Made National Products Factories Joint Association believes that this Industrial and Commercial Conference is of great importance to national product factories. Therefore, based on the opinions expressed by the factories of the association's members, the association is of the opinion that to promote the development of industry and commerce, all machine-made foreign-style commodity taxes and likin should be exempted first. The association, therefore, proposes that the machine-made foreign-style commodities should be exempted from all taxes and likin and that the raw material taxes should be refunded to maintain the national products industry. The proposal is jointly introduced by Xu Yongzuo, Pan Xulun, Jiang Wenyu, Huang Puqi, Zhang Zilian, and Zheng Shouzhi, members of the Industrial and Commercial Conference. The original text states: "The purpose of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the National Government in convening this Industrial and Commercial Conference is to discuss the removal of difficulties for industry and commerce, and promote the development of industry and commerce, so as to establish factories throughout the interior, and promote the improvement of industrial and commercial undertakings. The intention is good, and the whole country admires it. This association, as a large group of machine-made national product factories, hereby submits its daily experiences and difficulties, and believes that the decline of domestic industry and the stagnation of goods are due to the heavy burden of taxes and levies. The repeated imposition of taxes at every level is particularly painful for the circulation of goods in various parts of the country."

"The heavy taxation by customs and the repeated levies by likin offices cause merchants and travelers to hesitate, and goods to be stagnated. The number of factories in the interior are as few as the stars in the morning sky, and not only cannot they be expanded, but those already established are also closing down day by day. Taking cotton textiles as an example, from the import of raw materials to the production of cloth and its transportation to various places, there is a tax on foreign raw materials, a tax on the manufactured cotton yarn, a tax on the woven cloth, a tax on the local factory output, a tax from place A to place B, and a tax from place B to place C. In addition, there are taxes on machinery, taxes on dyes, taxes on fuel, taxes on decorations, and even taxes on auxiliary parts. This kind of complicated and chaotic tax system is not found in any other country in the world. Can Chinese goods compete with foreign goods? Failure is inevitable. Therefore, under this situation, Hua cotton and Hua yarn, woven into national cloth, bear different tax burdens because of the different cotton-producing regions. In some cases, the tax on Hua cotton is even heavier, and foreign cotton is more advantageous. As a result, Hua cotton, which is of better quality, is replaced by foreign cotton to reduce the cost of goods, causing agricultural products to accumulate and farmers to suffer. Is this not the fault of heavy taxes? The tax on foreign cotton and foreign yarn woven into national cloth is lighter, and the imported foreign cloth has no important surcharges in its own country. China only pays a customs duty of 5% ad valorem, plus a 2.5% surtax, which is the least advantageous. If the tax is calculated on a per unit basis, the assessed value is less than one-third. The comparison of Chinese and foreign tax rates is so disparate that it is already difficult for Chinese industry and commerce to compete with foreign countries. Moreover, foreign industries have more machines and fewer workers, resulting in mass production and achieving twice the result with half the effort everywhere. For example, the Toyota Yarn Factory in Japan has recently installed new-style machinery that allows one person to manage forty-five machines. Compared with China, where one person only manages two machines, the foreign labor cost, whether it is two or four times that of China, is vastly different. In terms of technology, under the lack of both talent and capital, the level of Chinese technology is undeniably immature and crude. The labor cost is not as low as others, and the technology is not as sophisticated as others. The government not only does not show sympathy but also wants to exploit it, imposing taxes at every pass and levies at every check point. To seek the development of industry and commerce is no different from heading south by driving the chariot north, going in the opposite direction. The decline of Chinese industry and commerce to this day, although affected by wars and banditry, is mainly due to the heavy burden of taxes and levies. Now that the wars are over and everything is starting anew, the National Industrial and Commercial Conference is convened at this time. The pain and difficulties of industry and commerce cannot be relieved without starting with taxes and levies. First, all taxes and likin should be abolished. All machine-made foreign-style goods, no matter where, should be exempted from taxation. The imported raw materials have already been taxed once, and the products are taxed again. One item is taxed multiple times, and the cost is more expensive than imported finished products. In this case, even if those who are enthusiastic about national products exhaust their efforts and resist foreign goods, what is the use? Therefore, the refund of raw material taxes will not only save domestic production and resist imports but also reduce costs and facilitate the sale of national products. After the exemption of all taxes and likin, any product, not limited to one place or one factory, can be manufactured anywhere and circulated at any time. In terms of technology, one can specialize in one aspect and achieve the benefits of division of labor and cooperation. For example, in Japan, the hygiene shirt factories are divided into different factories for spinning, weaving, dyeing, and finishing. Each factory specializes in manufacturing, and those who do not need to sell have separate sales organizations. The low cost and sophisticated technology are renowned throughout the country. The products are not only circulated in the country but also supplied to foreign markets. Why can't China imitate this? Furthermore, recently, the government, mindful of the depression of various industries, has heard of relief measures from time to time, such as cigarettes, matches, silk, and soap. With the recent silk industry, it has been nurtured and protected with all its might. However, instead of passively rescuing after the fact, it is better to actively support it beforehand. The method of exempting all taxes and likin and refunding raw material taxes is the only way to strengthen national power, relieve people's livelihood, and develop industry and commerce. The only hope for saving the dying vitality of the national industry and commerce is this. In addition to providing a separate explanation of the comparison of various tax systems, the outline of the proposal is listed as follows. Please include it in the agenda of commercial tax matters and quickly submit it for decision."

All Matters Related to Public Training of Citizens Are Handled by the Citizen Training Association

The Directors of Public Training in All Districts Are All Dismissed

The Municipal Executive Committee Notifies All Districts to Comply

The Shanghai Special City Party Executive Committee issued Instruction No. 186 yesterday, instructing the executive committees of all district party departments to immediately dismiss the Directors of Public Training. All matters related to public training in all districts shall be directly handled by the Citizen Training Association to unify authority and comply with the law. The instruction states: "For the sake of implementation, the position of the Director of Public Training in the party committees of various districts of this city is not only confusing but also has no legal basis. The 57th Standing Committee meeting of this Committee has resolved to abolish it. The executive committees of the relevant districts are hereby ordered to immediately comply with the abolition and conclude all files of the Public Training Committee. The various seals, together with the report books, should still be reported to the Public Training Association of this Committee. Hereafter, all matters within the scope of public training in the respective districts will be directly managed by the Public Training Association of this Committee."

Taxpayers' Association Opposes Increased Water Prices—Correspondence

Zhu Yicai's Reply to the Taxpayers' Association: "Respectfully acknowledging receipt of your letter of the 18th, I have fully understood its contents. Regarding the water fee issue of Deyuan Lane, I have previously agreed on terms with the tenants. Therefore, there was an established practice of collecting 1% along with the rent. The notice issued by my agent is to add 1.5%, which is based on the previous practice. However, the added amount will be temporarily kept separate. Before the Shanghai Real Estate Association issues a notice recognizing the increase, I will not lightly pay it to the water company. The reason for collecting the full amount from the tenants at this time is that I fear that when the matter is resolved in the future, it will be a long time since the start of the increase, and there are many tenants, so it will be difficult to collect the full amount due to possible relocation or other reasons. As Chinese citizens, how can I be willing to send the tenants' money to foreigners for no reason? I only hope that your Association can argue forcefully and achieve the cancellation of the water company's price increase. Then, the added 1.5% will be refunded to the tenants in full, and the tenants will not suffer any losses. Please convey my regards to the tenants of Deyuan Lane and hope that you will not publish this in the newspapers." Zhu Yicai, Shanghai Concession Chinese Ratepayers Association, 22nd of October, 1920.

The Taxpayers' Association to Zhu Yicai: "Respectfully acknowledging receipt of your kind reply today, I am deeply impressed by your explanation regarding the collection of water fees with the rent of Deyuan Lane as a kind of preparation. However, the amount of 1% is only mentioned in the notice as 2.5% for collecting the water price, and it is not clearly stated separately, which is misleading. Although the use of increased water prices is only related to your good offices, there is no need for our association to worry about it on your behalf. However, it is an ancient teaching to be kind to others. It seems that you should be asked to correct it. As for publishing it in the newspapers, the original intention was to let the public be aware of it. As for your upright actions, in your modesty, you do not seek fame, but the public is willing to hear it and regard it as an example. I am writing to you accordingly, hoping you will understand."

Silk Factories in Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Shanghai Have Decided to Issue Bonds

Nine Representatives Appointed to Petition in Beijing

At 5:00 PM yesterday, the Silk Industry Relief Special Committee held its third general meeting at the Silk Industry Association on North Xizang Road. After the ceremony, the chairman delivered an opening speech, mainly about requesting the issuance of bonds, hoping that the representatives would report on the past and discuss the progress. Next, the representatives from each district reported on the situation of the previous resolutions being returned to the meeting of the same industry. Zhejiang representative Jiang Laixian had some questions about the repayment of bonds. After discussion, it was decided to proceed with the original resolution. Wuxi representative Qian Fenghao raised the issue of interest payment and repayment of principal for the bonds. After public discussion, it was decided that the principal would be repaid in installments from the date of issuance of the bonds, and the interest would decrease with the principal. Subsequently, Zhu Mouqian, Shen Huachen, Qian Fenghao, Huang Jinqen, Zhu Jing'an, were appointed as members of the review committee. Wang Xiaolai, Huang Jinqen, Qian Fenghao, Zhu Mouqian, Shen Huachen, Zhu Jing'an, Zhuang Laixian, Huang Jinfan, and Cheng Bingruo were appointed as nine committee members to petition in Beijing, petitioning Chairman Chiang, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to approve the issuance of bonds of 10 million yuan, secured by a levy of 20 taels per 100 catties of silk, to be repaid in 65 months. They were scheduled to depart from Shanghai on the night train on the 31st of this month. Travel expenses were temporarily advanced by each district with 500 yuan. The meeting adjourned at 8:00 PM.

Silk Factories Request Rent Reduction

The Junyi Company Takes the Lead in Accepting

The Shanghai Silk Factories Association believes that most of the silk factories in this city are rented, and there are few who build their own factory buildings. This year, the silk market has been sluggish, and silk sales in Europe and America have plummeted. All the silk factories in the city have suffered losses and are unable to support themselves. The number of factories that have stopped production is increasing daily. In order to reduce the burden, the factories had previously held a temporary meeting and proposed to send a letter to the landlords requesting a temporary reduction in rent to help them maintain their operations. The letter stated, in brief, that the factory rents of each silk factory are all based on contracts. Contracts are related to the law, and the law is inseparable from human sentiment. Therefore, customs can change the law, and the situation can change customs. Landlords and manufacturers are interdependent. At this time of silk industry devastation, the landlords must also be deeply concerned and hope to have remedies. Therefore, after deliberation by the same industry, from September 1st until the silk market has not recovered, all those who can barely start production will temporarily pay 80% of the original rent, and those who stop working will pay 50%. A few days ago, the Tongyi Silk Factory first received a reply from the landlord, Junyi Company, which stated: "We have received your letter, which details the difficulties of your factory's operations, which is indeed the actual situation. Our company sincerely accepts your request in the true spirit of mutual assistance. The period is from September to May of the 20th year. The eight percent for starting production and the five percent for stopping are based on the standard of starting or not. It is a matter of mutual assistance, and we sincerely reply." Seeing that this company is the first to agree to reduce the factory rent, not wanting to be behind others, and showing enthusiasm for mutual assistance, it can be a model for the whole city.

The Commercial Workers' Union Issues a Declaration on the Xin Case

The Commercial Workers' Union issued a declaration on the Xin Dingchang case, in which French sailors drowned Xin Dingchang, stating that the imperialists have long held unequal treaties in China as a protective shield, disregarding the lives of Chinese people and our national laws. As a result, countless inhumane tragedies have occurred. The blood of Zhang Xueliang has not yet dried, the shame of Song Mingsheng has not yet been cleared, and the tragedy of Xin Dingchang has come again. Looking back on the past, our hearts are filled with anger. As citizens under the banner of the revolution in a new China, we hope that our wise government will avenge our grievances to restore national rights and wash away our shame to revitalize the nation. Unexpectedly, national grievances have not been avenged, but sovereignty has been lost; national shame has not been washed away, but our compatriots have died. This time, Xin Dingchang was asking for money for crossing the river, and French sailors dared to rely on their strength to beat him, knocking Xin Dingchang, who was unarmed and unable to resist, into the river, causing him to perish with the waves. After the incident, the murderers left swaggeringly. Although the water police station investigated several times, they did not allow an on-site interrogation of the murderers due to the influence of the French navy. It is obvious that the French naval authorities intentionally shielded the murderers and fostered cruelty. Giving money for crossing the river is the price for labor. The French sailors refused to give it barbarically, revealing their ugly and illegal face, and instead brutally beat Xin Dingchang, knocking him into the river and leaving without looking back. The contempt of French imperialism for the lives of Chinese people has reached its extreme. For the sake of safeguarding national rights and the nation, we hereby lead all members of our union and swear to be the diplomatic backing, until we achieve the punishment of the murderers, compensation for the families of the victims, an apology to our government, and a solid guarantee that similar incidents will not happen again. We hereby declare."

The Public Training Association of Citizens Thoroughly Investigates the Inside Story of the Rickshaw Industry Dispute

Organizing a Trade Union is Not Permitted for Outsiders

Increasing Rickshaw Rent Will Affect Public Security

丨Remarks by the Standing Committee of the Association丨

Guomin News Agency reports that the dispute among rickshaw pullers in this city due to the increase in rickshaw rent has led to the simultaneous appearance of advertisements from two rickshaw pullers' unions in the newspapers, attacking each other. To understand the truth of the union and the case, the reporter of Guomin News Agency visited Chen Jun, a standing committee member of the Public Training Association of the Municipal Party Committee, yesterday to inquire about the Party Committee's opinion on the case. The following is a record of Mr. Chen's remarks: (Following is Mr. Chen's statement) "There are many rickshaw pullers in this city, and there has never been a group organization. Back in May of this year, 55 people, including Lu Liangbi, jointly presented a request to the Party Committee to organize a rickshaw pullers' union, claiming to lead the rickshaw workers in the city and set up a meeting place at No. 19 Shaoqing Lane, Lafayette Road, French Concession. At that time, after investigation by the Party Committee, it was found that the people who initiated the organization of the union were not purely workers in the industry. Fearing that once the union was approved, there would be opportunities for outsiders to manipulate and use it, the union was not approved. The case was shelved. Until September 12th, He Wushan and eight others initiated the organization of the Shanghai Rickshaw Pullers' Union, set up a meeting place in Xilinsi Temple, Xilin Heng Road, and also presented a request to the Party Committee for approval, claiming to represent the rickshaw workers in the city. At the time, a ruffian extorted a special donation of one corner per week from the trade union in the French Concession. The Party Committee considered that the two unions both claimed to represent the city, so there must be other reasons or even someone who wanted to use the organization of the union to achieve private goals. Therefore, it immediately sent people to investigate the truth and rejected the request. Unexpectedly, only a few days later, on September 16th, Meng Jinchen and 50 others jointly presented a request to the Party Committee to organize the Shanghai Rickshaw Workers' Union, with its communication address at No. 66 Jiuruli, Yongxing Road, Zhabei, also claiming to represent the rickshaw workers in the city. By this time, the Party Committee was fully aware that the people who came to the meeting one after another to request the organization of a trade union and claimed to be representatives of the city were all excuses and not true representatives of the workers in the industry. Moreover, rickshaw workers are generally poorly educated and have always been indifferent to group organizations. But suddenly, there are so many associations requesting organization one after another. It is obvious that outsiders want to rely on the trade union for other purposes. However, at this time of rising prices and increasing cost of living, the rickshaw workers' daily earnings, apart from paying the rickshaw rent, leave them little to live on, making it extremely difficult to live. If the capitalists increase the rickshaw rent again, it will inevitably be too much oppression. Some people even advocated that because the number of trams and cars in this city is gradually increasing and the rickshaw business is greatly reduced, they propose that the authorities reduce the issuance of rickshaw licenses to further reduce the number of vehicles and increase the rickshaw rent. This is also an inappropriate proposal, because most of the rickshaw workers in this city come from various counties in northern Jiangsu. Because there is no work to be done in the interior, they come to Shanghai to pull rickshaws to make a living. If the number of vehicles is reduced and the rent is increased, the number of unemployed people will inevitably increase, which will affect the public security of this city. In short, the Party Committee is committed to relieving the suffering of the masses and guiding them to a bright future. If true rickshaw workers legally request to organize a trade union, the Party Committee will approve and support it and guide it to become a formal legal entity. As for the truth of this dispute, the Party Committee has sent people to thoroughly investigate it. After the investigation is clear, it will be reported to the central government for instructions and handling."

Commodity Inspection Bureau Invites Industry Leaders to Discuss the New U.S. Tariff Today

Relieving Imported Chinese Goods

Methods to Increase Tariffs

Among the goods that China exports to the U.S. market, raw silk is the most important, followed by tung oil, wool, cotton, hog casings, fur, tea, lace, soybean oil, and egg products. According to U.S. statistics, these goods were worth a total of US$182.7 million in 1929, accounting for 4.1% of the total value of U.S. imports. Recently, due to the high value of gold and the low value of silver, foreign trade has already suffered intangible losses. The newly enacted U.S. tariff also seeks to increase tariffs on imported Chinese goods, which will have a significant impact on the future of commerce. The Industry and Commerce Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce in Shanghai had previously reported the situation to the ministry, requesting that the news of the U.S. newly enacted tariff be corrected. The ministry then ordered that the news should be communicated to all provincial and directly subordinate agencies, which in turn would inform the chambers of commerce. The ministry ordered that since it would take too long for the ministry to forward the case to the chambers of commerce in various regions, raw silk, tung oil, cotton, livestock products, and other commodities, which are commodities that the ministry has designated for inspection, and the commodity inspection bureaus in various regions have considerable research on the export quantity and value of these commodities, the bureaus can directly convene the merchants in the relevant industries in the nearby regions, Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau should also convene the merchants and conduct careful research and discussion, and submit the results to the ministry for review and approval. After receiving the letter from the Industry and Commerce Bureau, the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau decided to invite industry leaders in hides, lace, and egg products to a meeting at the bureau at 2:00 PM today (the 23rd) to discuss effective relief measures and to reply to the Industry and Commerce Bureau, requesting them to send representatives to the meeting at that time.

The Ministry of Finance Plans to Repay Bonds Due This Month

Nine Types of Principal and Interest Redeemed in October

Total Principal and Interest Payable is More Than Six Million Yuan

Among the domestic bonds and treasury bills issued by the Ministry of Finance in the past, nine types of bonds are due to be drawn and repaid and pay interest in October this year. The total principal payable is 4,661,400 yuan, and the interest payable is 1,775,780 yuan. The unredeemed bonds of the above nine types of bonds amount to 6,209,827.199 yuan. Now that the time for drawing and redeeming the principal and interest has arrived, the Ministry of Finance has collected all the funds for paying the principal and interest and remitted them to various banks for distribution. The names of the various bonds and treasury bills that are due to be repaid this month are listed below: (1) Reissued 25; (2) Tianjin Customs 25; (3) Cigarette Treasury Bills; (4) Reissued Cigarette; (5) Customs Treasury Bills; (6) Demobilization Treasury Bills; (7) Third Batch of Cigarettes; (8) Customs Short-Term; (9) Haihe Public Bonds. Due to the situation, the above ninth type of Haihe Public Bonds has not yet been fully raised, so the drawing and repayment of the principal due this time will be temporarily deferred. The interest payable is 182,400 yuan, which has been announced by the Ministry of Finance as usual.

The Rickshaw Pullers' Unrest is Expected to Calm Down

The rickshaw pullers in this city have recently been distributing leaflets and trying to resist due to the issue of rent increase. Now, with the mediation of a third party, the rickshaw owners have expressed their willingness to compromise. It is because the rickshaw owners have been affected by the high value of gold and the improvement of living standards. In September, they all decided to increase the rickshaw rent by one corner to maintain their business. However, due to the opposition from the rickshaw pullers and the public criticism, representatives of the rickshaw pullers came forward to negotiate and request a reduction. The rickshaw owners also knew the difficult situation and voluntarily agreed to reduce the rent by five cents. The rickshaw pullers' representatives also considered it satisfactory. From then on, the unrest that had been brewing is expected to be resolved.

Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities Orders Owners to Cancel Artesian Well Permits

In order to ensure the safety of water supply, the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities requires all property owners in the city who have drilled artesian wells to provide drinking water to residents to register for permits for rectification. Subsequent inspections will be carried out separately, and the Water Quality Testing Laboratory of the Health Bureau will be consulted to test the water quality. If the water quality does not meet the cleanliness standards, improvements will be urged. Those that cannot be improved will be urged to switch to tap water. It is understood that owners in Zhabei and Hunan who have complied with the regulations to use tap water include those in Chang'an Lane on Qiujiang Road, Jiuru Lane on Yongxing Road, Zongyu Lane, Tongji Lane on Tongji Road, Hongxing Lane on Menggu Road, Yuande Fang on Tiande Road, Tiande Fang, Huikang Lane on Gonghe Xin Road, and Sihe Lane on Lujiabang Road. All the artesian wells in these places have been abandoned, and the Bureau has sent letters to the owners to return the permits for cancellation.

Grain Industry: The Chinese Grain Trade Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce the day before yesterday, stating: "We hereby respectfully submit that, according to the 'Provisional Measures for Wheat Inspection by the Shanghai Agricultural Products Inspection Office of the Ministry of Agriculture and Mining,' the standard for the natural moisture content of wheat is 14%, and the limit for impurities is 3%. The implementation of the inspection period has been extended to October 20. After this date, all wheat arriving in Shanghai must undergo inspection. All wheat that fails the inspection must be improved. The fundamental solution should start at the place of origin. In addition to publishing notices and informing various guest merchants transporting wheat to Shanghai to pay attention to rectification, we also request your Chamber to send a letter to the chambers of commerce in the cities and counties of the wheat producing areas, informing the wheat merchants under their jurisdiction that the wheat they transport in the future must first be thoroughly rectified at the place of origin to prevent adulteration, cement impurities, and other fraudulent practices, so that the goods arriving in Shanghai will be exempt from various picky inspections. We implore your assistance in this matter."

Marriage Dispute Between Male and Female Employees of Meidi Bookstore and Beixin Bookstore

After Consummating Cohabitation and Entering a Marriage Contract

Lu Shijun Never Returned on Pretext

Yang Chenqing Was Already Heavily Pregnant

Filing a Criminal Lawsuit with the Court

Yang Chenqing, also known as Yang Liwen, a female employee of Meidi Bookstore on Fuzhou Road and a native of Wuxi, is in her early twenties, has a pretty face, and has received secondary education. She lives with her mother at No. 4 Peidel Lane, Caojia Bridge, Ximen. Miss Yang recently retained lawyer Lu Qi to file a lawsuit with the Special District Court, criminally accusing her fiancé Lu Shijun (age 22), a native of the same hometown and an editor at Beixin Bookstore.

Luring a Minor Woman

Fraudulently Marrying, Maliciously Abandoning, and Also Accusing His Father, Lu Mianru, Who Was the Presiding Officiant at the Time, and Chen Weiruo, Who Was the Matchmaker, So They Were Also Sued. And Colluded with His Father, Lu Mianru, to Preside Over the Wedding, and His Friend, Chen Weiruo, as a Matchmaker, Pretending to Enter a Marriage Contract, Fraudulently Claiming to Be Married, and Indulging in Lewdness. She Is Now Six Months Pregnant, and Fearing Interference from the School, They Moved Several Times, Thus Depleting All of the Plaintiff's Clothes and Cash. Finally, He Lured Her to the Defendant's Old Home in Wuxi for Many Days. This Showed That All the Plaintiff's Savings Had Been Exhausted. Then, When the Money Was Gone, the Love Waned. He Incited His Mother to Come Forward and Drive the Plaintiff Back to Shanghai. At First, He Still Yielded and Pretended to Stay Together. Then, He Planned to Abandon Her, Claiming to Go to Take an Exam, and Never Returned. Occasionally, There Were Empty Letters of Comfort, But Finally He Betrothed Another Woman Named Zhou, Making

The Plaintiff Heavily Pregnant

Unable to Become a Wife, and with No Way to Support Herself, in a Dilemma, She Has a Sense of Being Unable to Survive and Wanting to Die Without a Way. Nothing Is More Cruel Than This. Considering That the Plaintiff Is a Young and Weak Woman with an Unsteady Will, She Has Been Trampled Like This, Although It Can Be Said That She Brought It on Herself, What Can Be Said? However, Reason, Morality, Law, and Ethics Do Not Tolerate This Female Scoundrel. And in a Few Months, This Loveless Child Will Be Born Again. Even If It Is Not for the Sake of the Plaintiff's Life and Personality, It Is Also

To Act as a Warning Against Female Rights Violators

Therefore, This Lawsuit Is Filed. Please Ask Your Court to Sentence the Defendant Lu Shijun for Violations of Articles 244, 257, and 310 of the Criminal Law. The Second and Third Defendants, Lu Mianru and Chen Weiruo, Will Each Be Punished for Crimes Under Article 258 of the Same Law, and Order Lu Shijun to Pay the Plaintiff Lifetime Alimony and Damages of 15,000 Yuan." The Court, Based on the Lawsuit, Approved It and Issued an Order, Ordering the Arrest and Notification of Each Defendant, Who Should Report to the Court for Questioning at the Appointed Time. Yesterday Afternoon, The Time for the Trial of This Case Had Arrived. Judge Feng Shide Presided Over the Questioning in the Fifth Criminal Court. All Three Defendants Were Present for the Hearing. Only Lu Mianru Commissioned a Lawyer to Appear in Court. Then, The Plaintiff's Agent, Lawyer Lu Qi, Stood Up and Described the Case.

And Submitted the Engagement Agreement

To Avoid Any Future Disputes, This Is a Certificate. If I Break My Word, I Will Be Punished by Law. It Is Clearly Stated on All Sides and There Are No Objections. Signed by Lu Shijun. Witness: Wu Ziming.)" Then, The Plaintiff Yang Chenqing Testified. Yang Was Wearing a Dark Green Plaid Short Jacket and Was Heavily Pregnant. She Stood in the Witness Box,

Eloquently Narrating the Experience

And Said That At That Time, I Was Working as a Female Employee at Meidi Bookstore, and the Defendant Was an Editor at Beixin Bookstore. Because of Our Similar Professions, We Approached Each Other. Lu Then Proposed to Me and Stated That He Had No Wife. Seeing That His Will Was Quite Firm and That He Was Studying at the University of Law and Politics, I Agreed. So We Rented a House in Rihui Lane Near the University of Law and Politics and Lived Together. My Mother Also Learned of This at That Time and Expressed Her Approval. The Defendant Lu Shijun's Father, Mianru, Also Approved and Was Willing to Act as the Presiding Officiant. From Then On, All Daily Expenses Were Paid by Mianru on a Monthly Basis. Until Last Year, When We Returned to Wuxi with Shijun, I Learned That

He Had Already Engaged to a Woman Named Zhou

However, He Had Not Officially Married Her. Then We Returned to Shanghai. In April of This Year, Shijun Claimed That There Was a Big Exam at School, So He Left and Never Returned. The Daily Expenses Were Cut Off and He Abandoned Me. At First, There Was Frequent Correspondence, But Then There Was No Trace of Him. I Have Not Seen Him Since. Now I Am Six Months Pregnant and About to Give Birth. The Defendant Thinks That He Has Graduated from University and Is Heartlessly Ignoring Me. I Cannot Marry Another Person, Nor Do I Want to Live with the Defendant. My Family Is Poor. Please Order Him

The Defendant to Pay Living Expenses

So That I Can Barely Survive. Otherwise, Please Punish Him According to the Law." Then, Lu Mianru's Agent Lawyer Stood Up and Said That "My Client Is Currently in Wuxi and Will Arrive in Shanghai Around the End of This Month. Therefore, We Request an Adjournment. As for the First Defendant Lu Shijun, He Is Mianru's Son. He Left Without Saying Goodbye in March of This Year and There Is No Trace of Him. The Third Defendant Chen Weiruo Is Not Known to Him. Now the Court Sent Chen's Subpoena to Mianru's Residence. Since There Is No Way to Forward It, We Have Specially Returned the Subpoena. However, My Client Lu Mianru Had Engaged a Woman Named Zhou as Shijun's Wife in His Hometown in 1928. In the Spring of Last Year, Shijun Declared to His Father That He

Did Not Want to Marry a Woman from the Countryside

And Wanted to Enter Into an Engagement With the Plaintiff Yang in Shanghai. Therefore, The Father and Son Cut Ties. Therefore, How Shijun and Yang Developed Their Relationship Afterwards Is Unknown. However, Mianru Is An Old-Fashioned Person. He Cannot Cancel the Engagement With the Zhou Woman Who Has Already Been Engaged in the Countryside." Judge Feng Reviewed the Testimony and Then Ordered That the Case Be Adjourned and the Defendant Be Summoned to Appear for Questioning.
